\section*{6D SUGRA Bases --- Unimodular ($|\det|=1$)}

Total SUGRA bases: 1280 (from 622 distinct LST bases, $T_{\text{LST}} \in [61, 80]$).

Filters: NHC, $c(k) \leq 8$, $H_n \geq 0$. Deduplicated by graph invariants.

\textcolor{red}{Red} = attached external curve. $\scriptstyle [\#=n]$ = intersection number $n$.
$\Delta = H_{\text{charged}} - V + 29T - 273 \leq 0$.
